let's talk about the gameplay as it's

most questions about survive is the
biggest departure from the Metal Gear
series in terms of gameplay Rising was
pretty out there but this is on a whole

survive is a survival game you need to
manage your food and water intake as
well as scavenge materials to craft
weapons and gear it takes a lot of
inspiration from Fallout 4 as you'll be
picking up anything that isn't tied down
to the geometry and throwing it in your

all of it can be picked up and turned
into materials this not only helps with

weapons and armor but it also helps
create structures at base camp like mgs5
we have our own mother base called base
camp just like mother base our current
